[==================== Test Case #1 ====================]
Question: For the year 2010, calculate the percentage of white population relative to the race total population for each zipcode.
Pred JSON: {"operation": "Projection", "details": {"columns": ["zipcode", "white_to_race_total_percentage"]}, "children": [{"operation": "Math", "details": {"expression": "CASE WHEN race_total_population!= 0 THEN CAST(white AS REAL) / race_total_population * 100 ELSE 0 END", "alias": "white_to_race_total_percentage"}, "children": [{"operation": "Filter", "details": {"condition": "year = 2010"}, "children": [{"operation": "Scan", "details": {"table": "demographics"}, "children": []}]}]}]}
Gold JSON: {'operation': 'Projection', 'details': {'columns': ['zipcode', 'white_percentage']}, 'children': [{'operation': 'Math', 'details': {'expression': 'CASE WHEN race_total_population != 0 THEN CAST(white AS REAL) / race_total_population * 100 ELSE 0 END', 'alias': 'white_percentage'}, 'children': [{'operation': 'Filter', 'details': {'condition': 'year = 2010'}, 'children': [{'operation': 'Scan', 'details': {'table': 'demographics'}, 'children': []}]}]}]}
Pred SQL:  SELECT zipcode, white_to_race_total_percentage FROM demographics WHERE year = 2010;
Gold SQL:  SELECT zipcode, CASE WHEN race_total_population != 0 THEN CAST(white AS REAL) / race_total_population * 100 ELSE 0 END AS white_percentage FROM demographics WHERE year = 2010;
Execution Error: no such column: white_to_race_total_percentage
result: X ERROR

Pred JSON: {"operation": "Projection", "details": {"columns": ["year", "native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage"]}, "children": [{"operation": "Aggregation", "details": {"aggregates": ["CASE WHEN SUM(race_total_population)!= 0 THEN SUM(CAST(native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander AS REAL)) / SUM(race_total_population) * 100 ELSE 0 END AS native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage"], "groupby": ["year"]}, "children": [{"operation": "Scan", "details": {"table": "demographics"}, "children": []}]}]}
Gold JSON: {'operation': 'Projection', 'details': {'columns': ['year', 'native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage']}, 'children': [{'operation': 'Aggregation', 'details': {'aggregates': ['CASE WHEN SUM(race_total_population) != 0 THEN SUM(CAST(native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander AS REAL)) / SUM(race_total_population) * 100 ELSE 0 END AS native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage'], 'groupby': ['year']}, 'children': [{'operation': 'Scan', 'details': {'table': 'demographics'}, 'children': []}]}]}
Pred SQL:  SELECT year, native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage FROM demographics GROUP BY year;
Gold SQL:  SELECT year, CASE WHEN SUM(race_total_population) != 0 THEN SUM(CAST(native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander AS REAL)) / SUM(race_total_population) * 100 ELSE 0 END AS native_hawaiian_and_other_pacific_islander_to_race_total_population_percentage FROM demographics GROUP BY year;
